<h1 class="header"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Elton John</span>
</h1>
<div class="infobar" id="name-job-categories">
<a href="#soundtrack" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Soundtrack</span></a> <span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="#producer" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Producer</span></a> <span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="#music_department" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Music Department</span></a>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-bio-text">
<div class="name-trivia-bio-text">
<div class="inline" itemprop="description">
Sir Elton John is one of pop music's great survivors. Born 25 March, 1947, as Reginald Kenneth Dwight, he started to play the piano at the early age of four. At the age of 11, he won a scholarship to the Royal Academy of Music. His first band was called Bluesology. He later auditioned (unsuccessfully) as lead singer for the progressive rock bands <a href="/name/nm1072743?ref_=nm_ov_bio_lk1"></a>...            <span class="see-more inline nobr-only">
<a href="/name/nm0005056/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bio_sm">See full bio</a> »
            </span>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-born-info">
<h4 class="inline">Born:</h4>
<a href="/name/nm0005056/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bth_nm"> Reginald Kenneth Dwight
</a> <br/>
<time datetime="1947-3-25" itemprop="birthDate">
<a href="/search/name?birth_monthday=3-25&amp;refine=birth_monthday&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_monthday">March 25</a>, 
     
<a href="/search/name?birth_year=1947&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_year">1947</a>
</time>
            in
            <a href="/search/name?birth_place=Pinner%2C+Harrow%2C+Middlesex+%5Bnow+London%5D%2C+England%2C+UK&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_place">Pinner, Harrow, Middlesex [now London], England, UK</a>
</div>
</td>
<tr>

</a> </span>
<h2>Did You Know?</h2>
<div class="see-more inline canwrap" id="dyk-personal-quote">
<h4 class="inline">Personal Quote:</h4>
I'm so sad. This woman was the queen of disco and so much more. Her records sound as good today as they ever did. That she has never been inducted into the Rock and Roll Hall of Fame is a total disgrace, especially when I see the second-rate talent that has been inducted. She is a great friend to me and to the Elton John AIDS Foundation and I will miss her greatly. (On <a href="/name/nm0838595?ref_=nm_dyk_qt1">Donna Summer</a>)                    <span class="see-more inline">
<a href="/name/nm0005056/bio?ref_=nm_dyk_qt_sm#quotes">See more</a>
</span>
                    »
        </div>
<hr/>
<div class="see-more inline canwrap" id="dyk-trivia">
<h4 class="inline">Trivia:</h4>
When <a href="/name/nm0005566?ref_=nm_dyk_trv1">Steve Winwood</a> left the <a href="/name/nm1363559?ref_=nm_dyk_trv2">Spencer Davis Group</a> to form <a href="/name/nm0870605?ref_=nm_dyk_trv3">Traffic</a>, he auditioned to take Winwood's place. Unfortunately, he was turned down.                    <span class="see-more inline">
<a href="/name/nm0005056/bio?ref_=nm_dyk_trv_sm#trivia">See more</a>
</span>
                    »
        </div>
<hr/>
<div class="see-more inline canwrap" id="dyk-trademark">
<h4 class="inline">Trademark:</h4>
Rich falsetto voice                    <span class="see-more inline">
<a href="/name/nm0005056/bio?ref_=nm_dyk_tm_sm#trademark">See more</a>
</span>
                    »
        </div>
